behavior slice_kiwi_and_add_to_cup(kiwi: item, cup: item, cutting_board: item, knife: item):
    body:
        achieve_once close_char(char, cutting_board)
        # Ensure character is close to the cutting board before slicing
        achieve_once inhand(knife)
        # Ensure knife is in hand to perform the slicing
        achieve_once on(kiwi, cutting_board)
        # Ensure kiwi is placed on the cutting board before slicing
        achieve cut(kiwi)
        # Slice the kiwi
        achieve_once inside(kiwi, cup)
        # Add sliced kiwi into the cup

behavior slice_kiwi(kiwi:item, cutting_board:item, knife:item):
    body:
        achieve_once close_char(char, cutting_board)
        # Ensure character is close to the cutting board before slicing
        achieve_once inhand(knife)
        # Ensure knife is in hand to perform the slicing
        achieve_once on(kiwi, cutting_board)
        # Ensure kiwi is placed on the cutting board before slicing
        achieve cut(kiwi)

behavior add_slices_to_cup(kiwi:item, cup:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(kiwi, cup)
        # Place the sliced kiwi inside the cup

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind kiwi: item where:
            is_food_kiwi(kiwi)
        # Select a kiwi
        bind knife: item where:
            is_knife(knife)
        # Select a knife
        bind cutting_board: item where:
            is_cutting_board(cutting_board)
        # Select a cutting board
        bind cup: item where:
            is_cup(cup) and has_water(cup)
        # Select a cup that already has water
        slice_kiwi(kiwi, cutting_board, knife)
        add_slices_to_cup(kiwi, cup)

#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_kiwi_2027_around_dresser_108(food_kiwi:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_kiwi)
    body:
        assert is_food_kiwi(food_kiwi)
        bind dresser_instance:item where:
            is_dresser(dresser_instance) and id[dresser_instance]==108
        achieve close_char(char,dresser_instance)
        if can_open(dresser_instance):
            achieve_once open(dresser_instance)
            exp(food_kiwi,dresser_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_kiwi,dresser_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_kiwi]=False
        close[food_kiwi,dresser_instance]=True
        close[dresser_instance,food_kiwi]=True
    

behavior find_food_fruit_2023_around_dishwasher_1001(food_fruit:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_fruit)
    body:
        assert is_food_fruit(food_fruit)
        bind dishwasher_instance:item where:
            is_dishwasher(dishwasher_instance) and id[dishwasher_instance]==1001
        achieve close_char(char,dishwasher_instance)
        if can_open(dishwasher_instance):
            achieve_once open(dishwasher_instance)
            exp(food_fruit,dishwasher_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_fruit,dishwasher_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_fruit]=False
        close[food_fruit,dishwasher_instance]=True
        close[dishwasher_instance,food_fruit]=True
    

behavior find_plate_1000_around_dishwasher_1001(plate:item):
    goal: not unknown(plate)
    body:
        assert is_plate(plate)
        bind dishwasher_instance:item where:
            is_dishwasher(dishwasher_instance) and id[dishwasher_instance]==1001
        achieve close_char(char,dishwasher_instance)
        if can_open(dishwasher_instance):
            achieve_once open(dishwasher_instance)
            exp(plate,dishwasher_instance)
        else:
            exp(plate,dishwasher_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[plate]=False
        close[plate,dishwasher_instance]=True
        close[dishwasher_instance,plate]=True

behavior slice_kiwi(kiwi:item, cutting_board:item, knife:item):
    body:
        achieve_once close_char(char, cutting_board)
        # Ensure character is close to the cutting board before slicing
        achieve_once inhand(knife)
        # Ensure the knife is in hand to perform the slicing
        achieve_once on(kiwi, cutting_board)
        # Ensure the kiwi is placed on the cutting board before slicing
        achieve cut(kiwi)

behavior add_kiwi_to_cup(kiwi:item, cup:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(kiwi, cup)
        # Place the kiwi slices inside the cup

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind knife: item where:
            is_knife(knife)
        # Select a knife
        bind cutting_board: item where:
            is_cutting_board(cutting_board)
        # Select a cutting board
        bind kiwi: item where:
            is_food_kiwi(kiwi)
        # Select the kiwi
        bind cup: item where:
            is_cup(cup)
        # Select the cup
        slice_kiwi(kiwi, cutting_board, knife)
        add_kiwi_to_cup(kiwi, cup)

behavior slice_and_add_kiwi(kiwi:item, cup:item, knife:item, cutting_board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once close_char(char, cutting_board)
        # Ensure character is close to the cutting board before slicing
        achieve_once on(kiwi, cutting_board)
        # Ensure kiwi is on the cutting board before slicing
        achieve_once inhand(knife)
        # Ensure knife is in hand for slicing
        achieve cut(kiwi)
        # Cut the kiwi
        achieve_once inside(kiwi, cup)
        # Add the sliced kiwi into the cup
